<p>苏莱曼大帝的遗产并不仅仅局限在军事领域。苏莱曼大帝归真一个世纪后，<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%95%E5%9B%BD" title="法国">法国</a><a class="mw-redirect mw-disambig" href="/wiki/%E6%97%85%E8%A1%8C%E5%AE%B6" title="旅行家">旅行家</a><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Jean de Thévenot" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="让·德泰弗诺"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%AE%A9%C2%B7%E5%BE%B7%E6%B3%B0%E5%BC%97%E8%AF%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="让·德泰弗诺（页面不存在）">让·德泰弗诺</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jean_de_Th%C3%A9venot" title="en:Jean de Thévenot"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Jean de Thévenot</span></a></span>）</span></span>亲眼目睹了“这个国家雄厚的农业基础、农民的幸福生活、充裕的主食和苏莱曼超群的政府编制。”<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79"><a href="#cite_note-79">[73]</a></sup> 苏莱曼对行政和立法体系的改革使他赢得了“卡努尼”（“立法者”）的称号，保证了他身后的帝国国祚长久，这一成就“足够让他之后的很多代颓废的后继者坐吃山空了”<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80"><a href="#cite_note-80">[74]</a></sup>。
</p><p>由于苏莱曼个人对文化的资助，奥斯曼帝国的<a href="/wiki/%E9%BB%84%E9%87%91%E6%97%B6%E4%BB%A3" title="黄金时代">黄金时代</a>在他的主持下拉开序幕。苏莱曼时代，奥斯曼土耳其人在<a href="/wiki/%E5%BB%BA%E7%AD%91" title="建筑">建筑</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%96%87%E5%AD%A6" title="文学">文学</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%89%BA%E6%9C%AF" title="艺术">艺术</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A5%9E%E5%AD%A6" title="神学">神学</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%93%B2%E5%AD%A6" title="哲学">哲学</a>等领域的文化成就达到了顶峰<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-atil24_7-1"><a href="#cite_note-atil24-7">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81"><a href="#cite_note-81">[75]</a></sup>。如今，<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%9A%E6%96%AF%E6%99%AE%E9%B2%81%E6%96%AF%E6%B5%B7%E5%B3%A1" title="博斯普鲁斯海峡">博斯普鲁斯海峡</a>、以及现代土耳其与前奥斯曼行省的很多城市的地平线上仍然装饰着<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A7%91%E6%9F%A5%C2%B7%E7%B1%B3%E9%A6%AC%E7%88%BE%C2%B7%E5%B8%8C%E5%8D%97" title="科查·米马尔·希南">科查·米马尔·希南</a>的建筑作品。其中，<a href="/wiki/%E8%8B%8F%E8%8E%B1%E6%9B%BC%E5%B0%BC%E8%80%B6%E6%B8%85%E7%9C%9F%E5%AF%BA" title="苏莱曼尼耶清真寺">苏莱曼尼耶清真寺</a>是苏莱曼大帝与他的妻子<a href="/wiki/%E8%AE%B8%E8%95%BE%E5%A7%86%E8%8B%8F%E4%B8%B9" title="许蕾姆苏丹">许蕾姆苏丹</a>的最终归宿，他们被葬在清真寺内的两座分开的陵墓中<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82"><a href="#cite_note-82">[76]</a></sup>。
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mosque_in_Mariupol.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1536" data-file-width="2048" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Mosque_in_Mariupol.jpg/220px-Mosque_in_Mariupol.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Mosque_in_Mariupol.jpg/330px-Mosque_in_Mariupol.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Mosque_in_Mariupol.jpg/440px-Mosque_in_Mariupol.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mosque_in_Mariupol.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a href="/wiki/%E4%B9%8C%E5%85%8B%E5%85%B0" title="乌克兰">乌克兰</a><a href="/wiki/%E9%A9%AC%E9%87%8C%E4%B9%8C%E6%B3%A2%E5%B0%94" title="马里乌波尔">马里乌波尔</a>清真寺</div></div></div>
<p>2007年，为了纪念苏莱曼大帝和他的<a href="/wiki/%E4%B9%8C%E5%85%8B%E5%85%B0" title="乌克兰">乌克兰</a>妻子<a href="/wiki/%E8%AE%B8%E8%95%BE%E5%A7%86%E8%8B%8F%E4%B8%B9" title="许蕾姆苏丹">许蕾姆苏丹</a>，乌克兰的<a href="/wiki/%E9%A9%AC%E9%87%8C%E4%B9%8C%E6%B3%A2%E5%B0%94" title="马里乌波尔">马里乌波尔</a>建造起一座<a href="/wiki/%E6%B8%85%E7%9C%9F%E5%AF%BA" title="清真寺">清真寺</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83"><a href="#cite_note-83">[77]</a></sup>。清真寺的建造者是土耳其商人萨利赫·吉汉，他和苏莱曼大帝一样出生于<a href="/wiki/%E7%89%B9%E6%8B%89%E5%B8%83%E5%AE%97" title="特拉布宗">特拉布宗</a>。每周五（<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%BB%E9%BA%BB%E6%97%A5" title="主麻日">主麻日</a>），当地的<a href="/wiki/%E7%A9%86%E6%96%AF%E6%9E%97" title="穆斯林">穆斯林</a>会去清真寺作<a href="/wiki/%E7%A4%BC%E6%8B%9C_(%E4%BC%8A%E6%96%AF%E5%85%B0%E6%95%99)" title="礼拜 (伊斯兰教)">礼拜</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84"><a href="#cite_note-84">[78]</a></sup>。
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<h2><span id=".E6.B3.A8.E9.87.8A"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="注释">注释</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%8B%8F%E8%8E%B1%E6%9B%BC%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%96_(%E5%A5%A5%E6%96%AF%E6%9B%BC%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="编辑章节：注释">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div id="references-NoteFoot"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-2"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-2">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">奥斯曼帝国苏丹自<a href="/wiki/%E5%A1%9E%E5%88%A9%E5%A7%86%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%96" title="塞利姆一世">塞利姆一世</a>起接受<a href="/wiki/%E5%BC%80%E7%BD%97" title="开罗">开罗</a><a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E6%8B%94%E6%96%AF%E7%8E%8B%E6%9C%9D" title="阿拔斯王朝">阿拔斯王朝</a>献出的<a href="/wiki/%E5%93%88%E9%87%8C%E5%8F%91" title="哈里发">哈里发</a>称号。</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-westname-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-westname_3-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">其他语言中的“苏莱曼大帝”还有：阿拉伯语：<span dir="rtl" lang="ar">سليمان العظيم</span>‎，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B3%A2%E6%96%AF%E8%AA%9E" title="波斯语">波斯语</a>：<span dir="rtl" lang="fa">سلیمان کبیر或سلیمان قدرتمند</span>‎，<a href="/wiki/%E4%B9%8C%E5%B0%94%E9%83%BD%E8%AF%AD" title="乌尔都语">乌尔都语</a>：<span lang="ur">سلیمان اعظم</span>‎‎，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B8%8C%E8%87%98%E8%AA%9E" title="希腊语">希腊语</a>：<span lang="el">Σουλεϊμάν ο Μεγαλοπρεπής</span>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E6%B4%9B%E7%B6%AD%E5%B0%BC%E4%BA%9E%E8%AA%9E" title="斯洛维尼亚语">斯洛维尼亚语</a>：<span lang="sl">Sulejman Veličastni</span>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A1%9E%E7%88%BE%E7%B6%AD%E4%BA%9E%E8%AA%9E" title="塞尔维亚语">塞尔维亚语</a>：<span lang="sr">Сулејман Величанствени</span>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%83%8F%E5%85%8B%E8%98%AD%E8%AA%9E" title="乌克兰语">乌克兰语</a>：<span lang="uk">Сулейма́н Пи́шний</span>，<a href="/wiki/%E7%BE%85%E9%A6%AC%E5%B0%BC%E4%BA%9E%E8%AA%9E" title="罗马尼亚语">罗马尼亚语</a>：<span lang="ro">Soliman Magnificul</span>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E6%B4%9B%E4%BC%90%E5%85%8B%E8%AA%9E" title="斯洛伐克语">斯洛伐克语</a>：<span lang="sk">Sulejman Skvostný</span>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BF%9D%E5%8A%A0%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%9E%E8%AA%9E" title="保加利亚语">保加利亚语</a>：<span lang="bg">Сюлейман Великолепни</span>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B3%A2%E8%98%AD%E8%AA%9E" title="波兰语">波兰语</a>：<span lang="pl">Sulejman Wspaniały</span>，西班牙语：<span lang="es">Solimán el Magnífico</span>，德语：<span lang="de">Süleyman der Große或Süleyman der Prächtige</span>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BE%A9%E5%A4%A7%E5%88%A9%E8%AA%9E" title="义大利语">义大利语</a>：<span lang="it">Solimano il Magnifico</span>，法语：<span lang="fr">Soliman le Magnifique</span>，俄语：<span lang="ru">Сулейманом Великолепным</span>，葡萄牙语：<span lang="pt">Solimão o Magnífico</span>，英语：<span lang="en">Suleiman the Magnificent</span>，日语：<span lang="ja">スレイマン大帝</span>等。</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-eastname-5"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-eastname_5-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">其他语言中的“苏莱曼大帝”还有：波斯文、普什图文、乌尔都文：<span lang="fa">سلطان سلیمان قانونی</span>‎等。</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-45"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-45">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">英文版：<i><span lang="en">Everyone aims at the same meaning, but many are the versions of the story.</span></i></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-sultan-53"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-sultan_53-0"><sup><b>5.0</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-sultan_53-1"><sup><b>5.1</b></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">土耳其语不分阴阳性，许蕾姆的“苏丹”头衔与苏莱曼大帝的“<a href="/wiki/%E8%8B%8F%E4%B8%B9_(%E7%A7%B0%E8%B0%93)" title="苏丹 (称谓)">苏丹</a>”头衔不同，后者相当于阳性（<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B7%E6%80%A7" title="男性">男性</a>）的苏丹，而前者相当于阴性（<a href="/wiki/%E5%A5%B3%E6%80%A7" title="女性">女性</a>）的苏丹，是（男性）苏丹之妻的称号（帝国早期苏丹之妻称“<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%AF%E6%95%A6" title="可敦">可敦</a>”），亦相当于“<a href="/wiki/%E7%9A%87%E5%90%8E" title="皇后">皇后</a>”。另外，苏丹的女儿也拥有（女性）“苏丹”称号，相当于<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E4%B8%BB" title="公主">公主</a>。</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-56"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-56">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">阿戈斯蒂诺从未见过苏莱曼大帝，但他在<a href="/wiki/%E5%A8%81%E5%B0%BC%E6%96%AF" title="威尼斯">威尼斯</a>可能见过画中的头盔并进行了<a href="/wiki/%E7%B4%A0%E6%8F%8F" title="素描">素描</a>。</span>
</li>
</ol></div>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.82.E8.80.83.E4.BE.86.E6.BA.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参考来源">参考来源</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%8B%8F%E8%8E%B1%E6%9B%BC%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%96_(%E5%A5%A5%E6%96%AF%E6%9B%BC%E5%B8%9D%E5%9B%BD)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="编辑章节：参考来源">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist columns references-column-count references-column-count-2" style="-moz-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2; column-count: 2; list-style-type: decimal;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-cihai-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-cihai_1-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="#CITEREF辞海1999">辞海 1999</a>，第691页："<span lang="zh-cn">苏里曼一世</span>"</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-4">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="#CITEREFMerriman1944">Merriman 1944</a>，<a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/in.ernet.dli.2015.87496" rel="nofollow">扉页</a></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-6"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-6">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="#CITEREFMansel1998">Mansel 1998</a>，第61页</span>
</li>

<li id="cite_note-29"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-29">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="#CITEREFThe_Encyclopedia_of_World_History2001">The Encyclopedia of World History 2001</a>，第<a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/encyclopediaofwo0000unse_i2x5/page/351/mode/1up" rel="nofollow">351</a>页，IV. The Early Modern Period, 1500–1800 &gt; C. The Middle East and North Africa, 1500–1800 &gt; 2. The Middle East, 1501–1808 &gt; a. The Ottoman Empire &gt; 1. The Rise to World Empire："<span lang="en">1548–49 Suleyman's second Iranian campaign. The Ottomans occupied Tabriz and Azerbaijan again but withdrew. Their only territorial gains from two years of warfare were Van, which was organized as a province, and some forts in Georgia.</span>"</span>

<li id="cite_note-31"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-31">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="#CITEREFThe_Encyclopedia_of_World_History2001">The Encyclopedia of World History 2001</a>，第<a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/encyclopediaofwo0000unse_i2x5/page/351/mode/1up" rel="nofollow">351</a>页，IV. The Early Modern Period, 1500–1800 &gt; C. The Middle East and North Africa, 1500–1800 &gt; 2. The Middle East, 1501–1808 &gt; a. The Ottoman Empire &gt; 1. The Rise to World Empire："<span lang="en">1553–55 Suleyman's third Iranian campaign. His forces ravaged parts of Iran but failed to force a showdown with the shah's army, which withdrew into the mountains of Luristan. In the peace agreement signed at Amasya (May 29, 1555), the shah recognized the existing boundaries and promised to end his propaganda and raids into Ottoman territory.</span>"</span>

<li id="cite_note-Mansel,_84.-48"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-Mansel,_84._48-0"><sup><b>44.0</b></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-Mansel,_84._48-1"><sup><b>44.1</b></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="#CITEREFMansel1998">Mansel 1998</a>，第84页，诗句的英文版：

<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r61209892" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
<blockquote class="templatequote"><span lang="en">The people think of wealth and power as the greatest fate,<br/>
<p>But in this world a spell of health is the best state.<br/>
What men call sovereignty is a worldly strife and constant war;<br/>
</p>
Worship of God is the highest throne, the happiest of all estates.</span></blockquote></span>

<li id="cite_note-55"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-55">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="#CITEREFWomen_in_World_History_Curriculum_Showcase">Women in World History Curriculum Showcase</a>，诗句的英文版：
<blockquote><span lang="en">"Throne of my lonely niche, my wealth, my love, my moonlight.<br/>
<p>My most sincere friend, my confidant, my very existence, my Sultan, my one and only love.<br/>
The most beautiful among the beautiful…<br/>
My springtime, my merry faced love, my daytime, my sweetheart, laughing leaf…<br/>
My plants, my sweet, my rose, the one only who does not distress me in this world…<br/>
My Istanbul, my Caraman, the earth of my Anatolia<br/>
My Badakhshan, my Baghdad and Khorasan<br/>
My woman of the beautiful hair, my love of the slanted brow, my love of eyes full of mischief…<br/>
I'll sing your praises always<br/>
</p>
I, lover of the tormented heart, Muhibbi of the eyes full of tears, I am happy."</span></blockquote></span>
